8/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_App_Sinc.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn100@2020_3/2020/08/31/05-51-04-233_58848ee31e15a601.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_App_World.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn54@2020_2/2020/08/31/05-50-48-527_b67c2b27cf7bf908.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_App_Focus.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn34@2020_4/2020/08/31/05-50-47-503_58a4748f4ffbc36b.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_9.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn66@2020_4/2020/08/31/05-50-59-828_280f81651835dcb4.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn38@2020_3/2020/08/31/05-50-48-392_eba90f9119a86f71.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_6.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn37@2020_3/2020/08/31/05-51-05-995_166a905ffea9d588.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Nuheara_IQbud_Max_2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn91@2020_2/2020/08/31/05-50-49-748_3cb0713aacff448a.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598853041845},{"createdTime":"2020-08-31 13:50:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 13:50:41","title":"Logitech Folio Touch for iPad Pro review – turn your iPad Pro into a laptop","link":"https://the-gadgeteer.com/?p=304159","description":"\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304391\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"673\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-3.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-3-297x250.jpg 297w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-3-768x646.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p><strong>REVIEW</strong> – Since I bought my iPad Pro 11 inch last year, I have intended to use it as a laptop replacement while not at my desk.  I’ve tried various case/keyboard/mouse combinations, and all have been frustrating enough to not work for me.  The Apple Magic Keyboard for iPad seems perfect, but the high cost is prohibitive for an occasional-use device for me. Enter the Logitech Folio Touch for iPad Pro.  I’ve been using it the past few weeks, including for writing this review, and it’s so handy it will be permanently affixed to my iPad going forward!</p>\n<h2>What is it?</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304393\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"938\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-1.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-1-213x250.jpg 213w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-1-682x800.jpg 682w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-1-768x900.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The Logitech Folio Touch for iPad Pro is a backlit keyboard and trackpad case for the iPad Pro 11.  It offers similar functionality to the Apple Magic Keyboard for iPad, but at about half the cost.</p>\n<h2>What’s in the box?</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304392\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-2.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"546\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-2.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-2-300x205.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-2-768x524.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>In the box is the Logitech Folio Touch for iPad Pro and a welcome/instruction manual.</p>\n<h2>Hardware specs</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Height: 10.08 in (256 mm)</li>\n<li>Width: 7.56 in (192 mm)</li>\n<li>Depth: 0.83 in (21 mm)</li>\n<li>Weight: 22.79 oz (646 g)</li>\n<li>Compatible with: iPad Pro 11-inch 1st and 2nd generation</li>\n<li>Automatic adjustable backlit keyboards (white only, 16 brightness levels)</li>\n<li>Position modes: Type, View, Sketch, Read</li>\n<li>Viewing Angles: 20-60°</li>\n<li>Power and Connectivity: Powered and connected by iPad via the Smart Connector</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Design and features</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304394\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"1019\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-4.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-4-196x250.jpg 196w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-4-628x800.jpg 628w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-4-768x978.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The Logitech Folio Touch has a fabric exterior (very similar to the Microsoft Surface tablet series keyboard cases), which is nice to the touch.  In my review period it didn’t seem to pick up too much dirt, but that would be my biggest worry over time.  The magnetic clasp can be folded back out of the way while not in use, and attaches magnetically to the back side of the case so it’s not flopping around.  It also doubles as a holder for a stylus like the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Apple-MU8F2AM-A-Pencil-Generation/dp/B07K1WWBJK\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Apple Pencil</a> or the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Logitech-Crayon-iPad-6th-Mini/dp/B07JFP5G4L\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Logitech Crayon</a>.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304395\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-5.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"1026\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-5.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-5-195x250.jpg 195w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-5-624x800.jpg 624w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-5-768x985.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The camera cutout works perfectly for both the first and second generation iPad Pro 11 inch models.  The fit and finish was good all around, I couldn’t find any defects on the fabric or burrs on the plastic.  The plastic parts do give a bit of a cheap feel to what would otherwise seem more of a premium device.  They’re good quality plastic, but it does feel toy-like.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304396\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-6.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"521\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-6.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-6-300x195.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-6-768x500.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The volume buttons are easy to locate by touch (the power button is a bit harder to feel).  All feel like they are a bit harder to push than the native buttons on the iPad, but I quickly adjusted to giving it that tiny extra bit of pressure and it was a non-issue for me.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304397\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-7.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"564\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-7.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-7-300x212.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-7-768x541.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The smart connector pins deliver power to the keyboard and are the method of communication.  This is noticeably better than bluetooth based solutions that I’ve previously tried.  Not worrying about charging an extra device like a keyboard or having that charge fail while working is great.  The cutouts for the speakers and USB-C port were also excellent, I didn’t have any issues with any of my USB cables (some cases are too thick and block some cables from connecting properly).</p>\n<p>The iPad is easily pushed into this case, and is held quite securely once in.  To get it out, you have to peel away the soft rubbery plastic from a corner then pull it out.  I found the area by the camera to be the easiest, you can push a finger into the camera cutout to help push the iPad out.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304399\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-8.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-8.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-8-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-8-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The keyboard itself is very similar to any Apple keyboard, with a few iPad-specific tweaks.  Judging from pictures, it’s nearly identical to the Apple Magic Keyboard’s layout, with the addition of a row of function keys (most of which I find very useful).   These function keys can adjust the iPad’s brightness, the keyboard’s brightness, media controls and volume, as well as a few other functions.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304400\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-9.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-9.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-9-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-9-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The kickstand on the Logitech Folio Touch is well-built and adjusts from nearly fully upright to nearly fully laid back.  I found it to be great for any work or entertainment scenario on a flat surface, but like the similarly designed Surface Pro series stands it could be less than ideal for couch use on my legs.  It generally worked fine, but the stand is where the weight of the iPad is carried, and often needed to be hanging over my knees to stay in place and balanced.  Overall, this worked well for me once I got used to it, but there were some positions that work with a laptop but won’t work with the Logitech Folio Touch.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304401\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-10.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"653\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-10.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-10-300x245.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-10-768x627.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>There is an open space on the top of the case where you can store/charge an Apple Pencil – they attach magnetically to the top of the iPad, so this is a nice touch.  If you charge/store the Pencil there, when you close the case, the magnetic clasp secures it which is very handy (I’ve had the Pencil come off in bags or backpacks more often than it’s stayed in place on the iPad alone).</p>\n<h2>Installation and setup</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304402\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-12.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"558\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-12.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-12-300x209.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-12-768x536.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>Setup for the Logitech Folio Touch was pretty simple.  First, I had to download the Logitech Control app from the App Store and insert my iPad into the Logitech Folio Touch device.  Upon opening the app, I was immediately prompted to update the firmware for the keyboard.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304403\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-13.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"558\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-13.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-13-300x209.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-13-768x536.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>This update took only a minute or two, then I was able to start using the trackpad and keyboard.  Everything worked well out of the gate except for the keyboard backlighting, it turns out you have to be on iPad OS 13.6 to support this feature.  One iPad update later and everything was working as expected.  Trackpad control was very good, it felt native and intuitive, with no lag like on bluetooth mice I’d previously tested.</p>\n<p>I didn’t notice any significant difference to my daily battery use during the review period.  Given that most similar devices with built-in small batteries last for weeks, I’d bet the power drain is very minimal.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304404\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-15.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-15.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-15-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-15-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The keyboard itself has very shallow key travel (which is expected from a slim device/case), but I had no issues adjusting to typing on the keys.  They respond to light typing nicely (unlike my 2018 MacBook Pro, which you feel like you have to stab aggressively).  I typed most of this review on the Logitech Folio Touch and had no issues or complaints.  The function keys and the up/down arrow keys are tiny, but I had no problems using them when needed.  The keyboard deck is slightly recessed to avoid it touching the screen when closed.</p>\n<p>The one minor annoyance I had was the top left key, which acts as a Home key.  This is in the location of the Escape key on a normal keyboard, and I often hit it while working to instinctively invoke a menu and was surprised every time to be yanked out of whatever I was working on and dropped back on my Home screen.  This was even worse when using remote desktop tools: I would forget I was on an iPad while controlling a Windows PC, and then hit Escape and get taken to the iPad Home screen.  Apparently I use Escape fairly often, but I’m learning to adjust to this Escape-less world and I’m able to get things done without it.  I hope that remote desktop tools can re-map this key in the future, but I have a feeling that Logitech has built the function key to always act as Home, not sure if 3rd party developers will be able to ever “fix” it.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304405\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-16.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-16.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-16-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-16-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The Logitech Folio touch allows for other positions which basically involve folding the keyboard back partially (for watching media or using a stylus) or all the way (to simply use the iPad as a handheld ipad).  These all worked well, the keyboard and touchpad input reliably disables when folded back so you’re not getting keypresses while moving or holding it in these positions.</p>\n<p>The device doesn’t add a lot of extra size or weight to the iPad.  I like that the case fully protects the iPad, but I’d also like a more minimalist version where it attached simply via magnets.  This may be wishful thinking, maybe the adjustable stand needs the solid wraparound case for leverage.  The iPad does feel about twice as thick with the case, but unlike other heavier cases (like the Brydge Pro) I didn’t find myself removing it often for non-keyboard use.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304412\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-18.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"599\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-18.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-18-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-18-768x575.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The backlighting on the keys is well done.  I found it to be evenly-lit and very adjustable (Logitech boasts 16 different levels of lighting).  In bright rooms, the keys are easily readable without the backlighting.  There are no RGB options here, only white.  The lack of backlighting is something that’s turned me off to other various iPad keyboard options. I often use it on the couch while half-watching some rerun of Archer or Arrested Development, and even though I’m a fairly good typist it’s always nice to be able to see the keys, especially when they have seldom-used function options.</p>\n<p>The trackpad is good, with one slight complaint.  It is a good size, not as large as the most recent trackpads on Macbooks, but larger than expected for a small device.  I never felt cramped or out of room while using the trackpad.  Multi-touch gestures worked great every time.  The one slight issue I ran into is that the top-left corner of the trackpad can’t be clicked.  I’m not sure if this is a design flaw or just my unit, and I only ran into it a few times, but it was strange when I did.  Every other part of the trackpad feels the same, with a solid click when pressed.  The top-left corner simply can’t be pressed in at all.</p>\n<h2>What I like</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Solid keyboard capabilities</li>\n<li>Excellent trackpad</li>\n<li>Versatile modes of use</li>\n<li>Not a lot of bulk added</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>What I’d change</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Trackpad top left corner unclickable</li>\n<li>Attach via magnets instead of wraparound</li>\n<li>Option to fully remove the magnetic clasp/stylus holder</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Final thoughts</h2>\n<p>Overall, the Logitech Folio Touch is a great keyboard/trackpad case for the iPad Pro 11.  This device truly transformed my use of my iPad from a consumption-only device to a productive device.  The trade-offs (extra width and weight) to add a keyboard/trackpad/case/stand  are minimal.  The price makes it attractive as well, especially compared to Apple’s offerings.  I heartily recommend the Logitech Folio Touch to anyone looking for a laptop-like experience with their iPad!</p>\n<p><strong>Price:</strong> $159.99<br>\n<strong>Where to buy:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.logitech.com/en-us/product/folio-touch.920-009743.html\" target=\"_blank\">Logitech</a> and <a href=\"https://www.bestbuy.com/site/logitech-folio-touch-keyboard-case-for-apple-ipad-pro-11-1st-and-2nd-gen-graphite/6424436.p\" target=\"_blank\">Best Buy</a><br>\n<strong>Source:</strong> The sample for this review was provided by <a href=\"https://www.logitech.com/en-us\" target=\"_blank\">Logitech</a></p>\n  <p>Filed in categories: <a href=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/category/reviews/\" 0-57-513_4251d097913943c6.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-13.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn99@2020_5/2020/08/31/05-50-55-633_caaa73137246a558.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-15.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn56@2020_4/2020/08/31/05-50-52-601_b0d46c611e9a4652.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-16.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn8@2020_3/2020/08/31/05-50-51-189_8b2ae7d7bf5a3428.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/logitech-foliotouch-18.jpg":null},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598853041842},{"createdTime":"2020-08-31 13:50:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 13:50:41","title":"Brigii Y120 Pro Mini vacuum cleaner review","link":"https://the-gadgeteer.com/?p=304368","description":"\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304384\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_12-scaled-e1597673220550.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"568\" height=\"768\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_12-scaled-e1597673220550.jpg 568w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_12-scaled-e1597673220550-185x250.jpg 185w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 568px) 100vw, 568px\"></p>\n<p><strong>REVIEW</strong> – We have a new family member in our house!  After almost two years being dogless, we decided to adopt this time around and get a rescue dog.  In our case, a rescue puppy!  He is a terrier/chihuahua mix.  He is very different from our previous dogs which have all been shelties.  For one, he is only around six pounds and he has very short fur.   I am learning the joys of having a short furred dog, even a very small one.  I don’t get the tumbling tumbleweeds of fur I used to get with our shelties, but I get small short fine bits of fur everywhere.  My home office furniture is dark, and I also have a dark workout mat on the floor.  Both items show the fur easily.  So when the chance came to review this Brigii Mini Vacuum I jumped on it.  Let’s see how it handles the dog fur!</p>\n<h2>What is it?</h2>\n<p>The Brigii Y150 mini vacuum is exactly what it says.  It is a cordless (USB rechargeable) mini vacuum and blower.  One end sucks and the other end blows.  The supplied attachments can fit on either end.</p>\n<h2>What’s in the box?</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304372\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_2-scaled-e1597672815954.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<ul>\n<li>The mini vacuum – the filter is already installed and ready to go</li>\n<li>One user manual</li>\n<li>One long flexible extension attachment</li>\n<li>One nylon storage bag</li>\n<li>USB-C charging cord</li>\n<li>hand pump blower tool</li>\n<li>A single dual attachment that has a brush that can retract to provide a crevice nozzle</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Hardware specs</h2>\n<ul class=\"a-unordered-list a-vertical\">\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Suction:4KPa</span></span></li>\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Running time: ≈15minutes</span></span></li>\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Lithium battery: 2500 mAh</span></span></li>\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Max power: 80W</span></span></li>\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Charging time: ≈4 hours(green light at full charging)</span></span></li>\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Dimensions: 2.6×2.6×8.5in</span></span></li>\n<li><span class=\"a-list-item\"><span class=\"a-size-base\">Net weight:1lb</span></span></li>\n<li>washable HEPA filter</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Design and features</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304376\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_6-scaled-e1597672860521.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>The vacuum/blower comes apart in two pieces.  The bottom part (top item on the picture) contains the motor and the port where the air will blow out.  The top part (bottom part on the picture) contains the air filter.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304375\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_5-scaled-e1597672850700.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>To remove the air filter you simply unlock the two halves of the machine and then pull out the filter from the top part as shown above.  I like to note that the filter is a HEPA filter and is advertised as completely washable.  I have not washed mine yet.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304377\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_7-scaled-e1597672869341.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>I took a picture of the motor half of the unit so you could see the locking mechanism that holds the two pieces together.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304378\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_8-scaled-e1597672879800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>This is a picture of the top half that has the slock the locking tab goes into.  You can see the filter inserted into the top half.  It simply slides in.  It does not have any grooves it has to fit into.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304379\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_9-scaled-e1597672891117.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\"></p>\n<p>This is the picture of the top half of the vacuum.  This is the end that sucks.  The bottom half looks identical except you can see a small Phillips screw head in the middle.  There are no indicators to tell you which end is the blower and which end is the vacuum.  When you turn it on though, it is very easy to tell at that point.  The blowing end puts out a substantial amount of air and you can feel the suction from the opposite end.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304411\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_14-scaled-e1597685635405.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>The picture above shows the tool that can be used on the blower end.  Without the wide upper end, the slim nozzle helps to focus the air blowing out.  It is not as strong as a can of air would be, but it did do an excellent job of blowing the dust and particles off of my keyboard.  I have not used the widespread end.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304380\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_10-scaled-e1597672903260.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>I took a picture of the main tool I keep on the vacuum.    I love this crevice tool because it has a nice soft brush on the end I can use to pick up dust and dog hair off my desk and keyboard.</p>\n<h3>Setup</h3>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304373\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_3-scaled-e1597672829988.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>Setup was really easy.  I simply plugged the USB-C cable into the vacuum and put the USB cable into the side of my PC.  It took several hours to charge there, but my laptop does not put a lot of power out of its USB ports.  When I plugged it into a charger in an outlet it charged much faster.  While charging, it has an LED light on the power button that glows red.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304374\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_4-scaled-e1597672839950.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>When it is fully charged, the LED turns green.  One note, on the Amazon website where these are sold, people mention the red light blinking.  It never blinked for me.  It stayed a solid red color.  I also want to note that the Amazon page shows a small tube coming out of the blower end of the device.  I do not have one of those attachments.</p>\n<h3>Performance</h3>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304381\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Brigii_11-scaled-e1597672915419.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"800\"></p>\n<p>I really like the performance of this vacuum.  It is perfect for keeping my keyboard and desk area clean.  It also does a really good job of spot cleaning my exercise mat.  It picks up the small dog fur easily.  If we still had shelties I can imagine the filter would get clogged pretty easily.  The above picture shows the filter after about five, two-minute vacuum sessions around my office.  I saw where some folks talk about using this vacuum in their car.  I think it would be ok for something like that, and handy to have if you have children who tend to leave crumbs in the car, but I don’t think it can beat the shop vacuum that I always use when cleaning my car.</p>\n<p>It also holds its charge a long time.  I went a week without using it, and it still had plenty of power.    I used it probably 15 times doing quick pickups around my office before it needed a recharge.  Using it daily on my keyboard it easily lasted over a week.</p>\n<h2>What I like</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Small and portable</li>\n<li>cordless</li>\n<li>holds a charge for a long time.</li>\n<li>I love that the filter is washable.</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>What needs to be improved</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>It could use more suction power, but hey, I say that about almost any vacuum except my shop vac.</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Final thoughts</h2>\n<p>If you are looking for a small hand held cordless vacuum for small tasks like keeping your desk area clean including your keyboard, I highly recommend this product.  It does the job and it does it at a great price.  Do not buy this thinking you will vacuum out your entire car that you have not cleaned all year.  However, for spot jobs when your kid finishes eating a bunch of crackers, this should do the job.  Note, when shopping for this item, be sure you get the Pro version.  There is another version that is around $5 cheaper but it also has a smaller battery and does not come with the flexible hose.</p>\n<p><strong>Price</strong>: $39.99<br>\n<strong>Where to buy</strong>: <a href=\"https://amzn.to/3joNp6M\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">Amazon</a><br>\n<strong>Source</strong>: The sample of this product was provided by Brigii.</p>\n  <p>Filed in 13:50:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 13:50:41","title":"Toothshower 2.0 review","link":"https://the-gadgeteer.com/?p=304457","description":"\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full 100vw, 232px\"></p>\n<p><strong>REVIEW</strong> – I pay a lot of attention to the care of my teeth and I floss every day, twice daily. One thing that I hate about conventional flossing is that at times it makes my gums bleed. I have often thought about buying a Waterpik as an alternative but I never got around to it. I now get the opportunity to test the Toothshower 2.0. Let’s see how it goes.</p>\n<h2>What is it?</h2>\n<p>The Toothshower 2.0 offers an enhanced Open-air Handle Design and a more robust Magnetic Handle Cradle. It allows you to control water pressure on the console with an easy to turn Comfort Pressure Dial.  Additional accessory storage and/or travel-size toothpaste storage is available under the mirrored hood.</p>\n<h2>What’s in the box</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304498\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-2.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"450\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-2.jpg 450w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-2-188x250.jpg 188w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 450px) 100vw, 450px\"><br>\n1 x Toothshower 2.0<br>\n1 x Irrigating Standard Tip (White)<br>\n1 x Irrigating Gum Massager (White)<br>\n1 x Irrigating Dual-Headed Toothbrush (White)<br>\n1 x Wall Plate<br>\n1 x Custom Diverter<br>\n1 x Plumber’s Tape<br>\n1 x 3M Command Waterproof Cord Clip<br>\n3 x 3M Command Waterproof Bath Adhesive Strips<br>\n1 x User Manual</p>\n<h2>Design and features</h2>\n<h3>Features</h3>\n<ul>\n<li>\n<strong>EASY FLOSSING:</strong> For healthier gums, fresher breath, and happier teeth with less effort (Dentist and Dental Hygienist Approved) Customer Reviews.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>ATTACHES TO YOUR SHOWER:</strong> Saving counter space, no mess, endless water supply with no water reservoir to refill.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>NO BATTERY OR OUTLETS NEEDED:</strong> Powered by your shower with adjustable pressure dial, and shower-temperature control for comfort.</li>\n<li>\n<strong>INCLUDES MULTIPLE ACCESSORIES:</strong> Standard Water Flosser tip, irrigating Dual-Headed Toothbrush, and revolutionary 7-stream Gum Massager, which cleans around orthodontics and implants.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>The main section of the Toothshower 2.0 is made of plastic and comes with everything you need to use it. It has a built-in cradle for the handle, compartments for storing accessories, a mirror, and the wall mounting accessories. It also has a dial to control the water pressure.<br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304500\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"334\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-3.jpg 334w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-3-139x250.jpg 139w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 334px) 100vw, 334px\"><br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304501\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"307\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-4.jpg 307w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-4-128x250.jpg 128w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 307px) 100vw, 307px\"><br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304502\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-6.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"450\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-6.jpg 450w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-6-188x250.jpg 188w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 450px) 100vw, 450px\"><br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304530\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-20.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"513\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-20.jpg 513w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Toothshower-20-214x250.jpg 214w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 513px) 100vw, 513px\"></p>\n<h3>Performance</h3>\n<p>Before using the Toothshower, it has to be installed in the shower. The only connections that have to be made are the Diverter in between the shower pipe and showerhead and the hose from the Toothshower to the diverter.<br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter change</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Include additional adhesive strips should any get damaged during installation</li>\n<li>A cord clip with a larger surface to attach to the shower wall. Well, I will readily admit that I was wrong. This device is easy to install and after a few uses, I look forward to using it especially for flossing and gum massaging. The toothbrush also works well and the fact that it does not need batteries is fantastic. loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305356\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-5.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" know about me. I’m a stationery nerd. I love journals, pens, and washi tape. If you don’t know what washi tape is, they are small rolls of decorative tapes that come in different widths and designs. You can use these tapes to decorate your journal pages. I love them, but finding a way to store them and have them easily available can be a challenge. That’s where a washi tape dispenser like Walden Woodworkers holder from Galan Leather can really come in handy. Let’s take a look.</p>\n<h2>What is it?</h2>\n<p>The Galan Leather Washi Tape Dispenser is a vintage styled wooden and cast iron holder for standard MT washi tape rolls (1.5 cm width).</p>\n<h2>Design and features</h2>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305350\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-11.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-11.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-11-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-11-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>First of all, here’s a small selection of my washi tape collection.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305351\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-10.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"526\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-10.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-10-300x197.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-10-768x505.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The handmade Walden Woodworkers washi tape holder is available in either mahogany or walnut. The quality of the construction is wonderful. The wood is well finished with no splinters or rough edges. It reminds me of something you might see in a shop 100 years ago, especially with the brass plate on the front.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305352\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-9.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-9.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-9-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-9-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The dispenser has 3 parts. There’s the base which is made of wood held together with strong cast iron plates, a wooden dowel that holds the tapes, and a cutting blade.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305353\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-8.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-8.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-8-300x225.jpg 300w, shallow teeth.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305354\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-7.jpg\" alt=\"\" https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-7-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-7-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>To load the holder, you just lift out the wooden dowel, slide the tapes onto the dowel, and place it back in the holder.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305357\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"581\" https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-4-768x558.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The number of tapes that can fit on the 10 inch long dowel really depends on the washi tapes which come in a variety of widths.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305358\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-3-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>The design of this dispenser is simple and easy to use. Once loaded, you just unroll the tape you want to use and pull it across the cutting blade to cut it to your desired length.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305359\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-2.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-2.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-2-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-2-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>One thing to note is that the blade does leave the tape with a jagged edge that may or may not be to your liking.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-305355\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-6.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-6.jpg 800w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-6-300x225.jpg 300w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/galanleather-washi-6-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\"></p>\n<p>I was only able to load 18 rolls on my Walden Woodworkers washi tape dispenser and since I have a lot more tapes, I had to be selective. src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-2.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"450\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-2.jpg 450w, SleepScore Max was to follow the instructions and download the app making sure that both my Bluetooth and WiFi were turned on.<br>\n<strong>Important Note from Sleepscore:</strong><br>\nBefore you follow these set-up instructions, please ensure that<br>\nboth the Bluetooth and Wi-Fi are enabled on your Smartphone.<br>\nDo not power up your SleepScore Max until instructed to do so.</p>\n<p>Once you follow the directions via the app after you register, the pairing process is easy and much like most other devices that connect via Bluetooth. The placement of the device is very important:<br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304440\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-21.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"401\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-21.jpg 401w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-21-167x250.jpg 167w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 401px) 100vw, 401px\">Once set up, you open the app and do the following:<br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-304441\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-22.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"482\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-22.jpg 482w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Sleepscore-22-201x250.jpg 201w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 482px) 100vw, 482px\"><strong>According to Sleepscore:</strong><br>\nSleep is divided into various stages: <strong>light, deep, and REM (Rapid</strong><br>\n<strong>Eye Movement).</strong> A healthy combination of the three ensures a more<br>\nrestful and restorative sleep.<br>\n<strong>Light sleep</strong> takes up the majority of your sleep time and is important<br>\nfor the development of muscle memory. During this stage, your<br>\nbreathing becomes more regular and shallow as you transition into<br>\na deep sleep.<br>\nDuring <strong>deep sleep</strong>, many physical functions slow down, which is<br>\nnecessary to revitalize both the body and the immune system. During this<br>\nstage, your breathing rate is slowest and the most regular.<br>\n<strong>Rapid Eye Movement or REM</strong> is the period of sleep in which you<br>\ndream the most. Eye movements are rapid and random, memories are<br>\nstored and the brain is regenerated. During this stage, your breathing<br>\nbecomes more irregular as you process your dreams and your mind<br>\nrecharges.</p>\n<p>Screenshots from the app representing measurements:</p>\n\n<a 13:50:41","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 13:50:41","title":"Core Meditation Trainer review","link":"https://the-gadgeteer.com/?p=303633","description":"\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304086\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-13.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"600\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p><strong>REVIEW</strong> – I keep trying to do the meditation thing. I’ve tried apps, podcasts, devices… I always seem to have a tough time getting focused.  The Core Meditation Trainer takes a different approach to helping you find your inner peace, no experience required. Let’s find out if Bob is on the pathway to enlightenment. To the review!</p>\n<h2>What is it?</h2>\n<p>It’s an integrated device and app that combines a physical focus, haptic feedback, and ongoing measurement of your mental state to help you meditate. Please note that the app is only available for the iOS at the moment, but Android compatibility is in development.</p>\n<h2>What’s in the box?</h2>\n<p>You’ll get the Core trainer, a wall plug, a micro-USB cable, and a charging dock.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304089\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-16.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-16.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-16-250x250.jpg 250w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<h2>Hardware specs</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>USB charging dock</li>\n<li>Natural wood integrated into the design</li>\n<li>Custom haptic measurement system</li>\n<li>Bluetooth 4 enabled</li>\n<li>Device battery operates for up to two weeks between charges</li>\n<li>iOS app compatible (Android coming soon)</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Design and features</h2>\n<p>The Core Meditation Trainer is a softball-sized device that, when when paired with the app. integrates a physical component that both focuses your efforts and provides feedback on your progress. Meet your meditation orb.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304090\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-17.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-17.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-17-250x250.jpg 250w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p>It’s an elegant piece of design that uses real rosewood in the base. This makes it very pleasant to handle, which is important as you’ll be using it during every session.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304091\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-18.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-18.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-18-250x250.jpg 250w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p>The bottom of the orb is designed to sit in the base included in the package for charging. The unit can go up to two weeks between charges.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304092\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-19.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"404\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-19.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-19-300x202.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p>I really like the style &#38; elegance of the device. I have mine set up on my desk. Not only does it look great, but it’s always within easy reach if I want to do a quick meditation session between conference calls. Here I’ve connected the base with the included cable to the USB charging port on my desk lamp.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304093\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-20.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"424\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-20.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-20-300x212.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p>The orb serves as your focus when you are engaged in meditation sessions, using a series of rising and falling vibrations that match the pattern of the breathing for the program you’re running. While this is happening, the sensors are continually monitoring your biometrics (heart rate and heart rate variability, specifically) to report on your levels of calm and focus. Let’s do a session to see how this all comes together.</p>\n<h3>Meditation Sessions</h3>\n<p>We’ll walk through the app features shortly, but one of the clever bits about the Core Meditation Trainer is that there’s virtually no learning curve to get started. You don’t even need to select a meditation program. Launch the app and a program is automatically queued up for you, like so:</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304082\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-9-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-9-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-9-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-9.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>Or you can select a program from the library, like the one I am showing here.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304077\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-4-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-4-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-4-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-4.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>Either way you go, just find a place to get comfortable and sit with the orb in both hands.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304088\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-15.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-15.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-15-250x250.jpg 250w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p>Place your thumbs on the sensors, and the program automatically begins with a three second countdown.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304087\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-14.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-14.jpg 600w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-14-250x250.jpg 250w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"></p>\n<p>This particular program was a five minute session. The soundtrack is a layered ]audio experience that includes gentle music and sound effects that rise and falls in a steady rhythm. The orb vibrates in a synchronization to the soundtrack, intensifying as the audio swells and then falling back as it recedes. This becomes your focus to match the breathing patterns. It’s quite soothing.</p>\n<p>At the end of your session the app presents the results. It shows you your heart rate during and the levels of calm and focus you were able to maintain during the session.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304074\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-1-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-1-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-1-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-1.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>When you first start using the Core Meditation Trainer you’ll do a couple of sample sessions to collect some baseline biometrics. Heart rate and heart rate variability seem to be the key indicators that Core uses to determine dimensions like “calm” and “focus.” I’m not sure entirely how these calculated, but what’s interesting is that the Core starts to build a profile on you as you use it more often that shows your progress. You can see how stressed out you may have been today vs. other sessions, and get immediate feedback on the results for that exercise.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304075\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-2-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-2-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-2-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-2.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>You can also keep notes on your sessions for future reference, which is handy if you find a specific set of programs that you really like.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304076\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-3-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-3-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-3-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-3.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>As you collect more data Core builds a history of your progress, allowing you to keep tabs on your development. Training is a summary overview of your activity with the device.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304078\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-5-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-5-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-5-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-5.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"> <img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304079\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-6-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-6-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-6-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-6.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>Switch to the Calm and Focus reports, and you’ll learn how long you were able to maintain those states in each session and as an overall measurement against your time with the program.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304080\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-7-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-7-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-7-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-7.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>I found these metrics to be very helpful. You can see that I’ve got a lot to learn about focus (heh). But I also found it interesting to see that I got better results with longer sessions. I’ve seen better results in the last two weeks since I took these screenshots, but I still have a way to go!</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304081\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-8-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-8-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-8-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-8.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<h3>Additional App Features and Programs</h3>\n<p>When you start the Core will take you through a series of programs that give you a sampling of what’s available. It also runs you through some basic breathing exercises and trainings to prepare for what’s to come. When you’re ready to go deeper, the Explore option allows you to choose from dozens of different programs.</p>\n<p>The Guided programs are purpose-driven, organized by categories like “Productivity and Performance” and “Sleep” to enable sessions with specific mental/wellness goals. These are typically accompanied by an instructor that walks you through the program. Breath Training programs teach you different breathing methods to accomplish goals like stress relief and are also guided by an instructor. Sound programs are unguided audio soundscapes. In each case you get a full description of the session, and you can choose the length of the program. I snagged a sample of the “Coffee breathing”  program as an example. Pick that option from the menu.</p>\n<p> </p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304083\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-10-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-10-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-10-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-10.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>You can now choose to run the introductory exercise, or choose the session length if you’re familiar with it.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304084\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-11-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-11-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-11-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-11.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>Swipe up for a detailed description. In some cases you can select to add a backing audio track if you want a little more depth behind the instructor’s voiceover. It also explains the techniques you will use during the session.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304085\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-12-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-12-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-12-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-12.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>And if you REALLY want to explore more options, you can sign up for the Premium subscription service. These are sessions designed by expert meditation instructors covering a wide variety of topics and meditations. <img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304098\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-31-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-31-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-31-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-31.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>There are 15 different instructors as of this writing, and they create new programs that are added on a weekly basis. Extensive bios are also included on each instructor.</p>\n<p><img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304099\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-32-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-32-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-32-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-32.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>If you find an instructor whose style you like, you can run any program they have added to the app.<br>\n<img loading=\"lazy\" class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-304100\" src=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-33-370x800.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"370\" height=\"800\" srcset=\"https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-33-370x800.jpg 370w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-33-115x250.jpg 115w, https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-33.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px\"></p>\n<p>This combination of programs and new content (with the subscription) give you endless variety to work with based on your needs and goals.</p>\n<h3>Performance</h3>\n<p>I’m really impressed with how the Core Meditation Trainer presents a well-rounded user experience, especially for those of us who aren’t particularly good at this kind of stuff. You don’t need to be practiced at meditation to get results. I see three elements to the experience that really work seamlessly together: <strong>form factor</strong>, <strong>measurement</strong>, and <strong>customization</strong>,</p>\n<p>The <strong>form factor</strong> is on point. The orb is easy to handle and comfortable to hold for extended periods. I find it much easier to concentrate on the exercises when there is a physical element involved as a point of focus. I’m also finding that the responsive nature of the device is also critical to getting better results. My earlier sessions (shown above) weren’t as good because I kept trying to force my breathing patterns on the thing. When I learned to simply follow the vibrations my recent experiences have shown steady improvement. I also really like the simplicity of the interface. Pick it up, close your eyes, put your thumbs on the sensors, and off you go. It encourages more active use as I get breaks in my day or need a minute to calm things down.</p>\n<p><strong>Measurement</strong> is critical to improving performance in any activity. The Core does an excellent job of providing meaningful measurement without getting so complicated that you don’t know how to interpret the results. I may not know exactly how they calculate the metrics, but I don’t need to. I get immediate feedback after a session, and have the ability to measure performance over a time that demonstrates improvement in simple terms. That’s all good for encouraging use and re-use.</p>\n<p>Finally, there’s the <strong>customization</strong> element. You’re not locked into a specific meditation technique or fixed program here. You can try different techniques and tools to find what works for you, and change up the duration/variation to meet your schedule. The subscription service offers a wide range of instructors with different styles, so you can find one (or several) that you groove with to cater your programs to your liking. The wide variety of options available also encourages use and re-use as your needs change.</p>\n<p>I still have a ways to go to get good with this thing, but I’m enjoying the journey. And that’s half of the battle, right?</p>\n<h2>What I like</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Very user friendly, even if you are new to meditation</li>\n<li>Haptic feedback is excellent for focusing your efforts</li>\n<li>Excellent app with a wide variety of programs</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>What needs to be improved</h2>\n<ul>\n<li>Nothing that I am seeing so far</li>\n</ul>\n<h2>Final thoughts</h2>\n<p>I’ve tried a number of different apps &#38; devices related to meditation, but the Core Meditation Trainer is my favorite so far. It’s the first solution I’ve seen that combines quality content, haptic feedback and measurables in one well-rounded package. The form factor and experience are so good that you don’t even need to think about it… which is kind of the point. We’ll see how it works over the long haul.</p>\n<p><strong>Price</strong>: $169 for the unit, $59.99 annual fee for the Core Premium app subscription. Discount pricing available when you bundle the device &#38; subscription together.<br>\n<strong>Where to buy</strong>: Go to the <a href=\"https://hellocore.com/get-core\" target=\"_blank\">purchase page on the Core web site</a>.<br>\n<strong>Source</strong>: The sample of this product was provided by <a href=\"https://hellocore.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Core</a>.</p>\n  <p>Filed in categories: <a ainer-32-370x800.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn50@2020_4/2020/08/31/05-50-59-065_e92d65a850f9bfcb.webp","https://the-gadgeteer.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Core-MeditationTrainer-33-370x800.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn19@2020_5/2020/08/31/05-50-55-860_bd6d22a970379d9a.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598853041841},{"createdTime":"2020-08-31
